## IV. OUR NATURALLY INSEPARATING GEODESIC METHOD

---

### Reuniting

When we open any modern dictionary to "nature," we find humans excluded from the definition. Merriam-Webster: "the external world in its entirety." Oxford: "as opposed to humans or human creations." Cambridge: "independently of people." When we open the same dictionary to "human nature," we find nature inside humans. Merriam-Webster: "the fundamental dispositions and traits of humans." Oxford: "the essential quality of humankind." Cambridge: "the natural ways of behaving that most people share." The same dictionary carries both. Nature is outside humans. Nature is inside humans. Humans are nature inside nature.

Inside: human nature, the natural ways of behaving, the fundamental dispositions, the inherent sense of right and wrong. Outside: nature, the external world, the physical world, the plants and animals and forces. Persisting: the same word "nature" in both definitions, the same dictionary carrying both, every speaker using both daily. The word "human" is the membrane. Add "human" to nature and nature moves inside. Remove "human" from nature and nature moves outside. The membrane persists.

The separation of humans from nature is installed in the primary definition and contradicted by the same dictionary's definition of human nature. Every one-way description in science, technology, and common language inherits this separation. Dissolve the separation and humans are nature inside nature and every one-way description resolves into both directions alive through each other.

Webster's 1828, the oldest standard dictionary, carries no contradiction: "whatever is made or produced; a word that comprehends all the works of God; the universe." Humans are inside. The separation was installed later. The OED labelled the human-including definition obsolete and removed the obsolete label in April 2024. The including definition was declared dead and brought back to living.

The dictionary definitions of nature, science, and technology contain zero coupling between them. Nature does not contain the word science or technology. Science does not contain the word nature except as adjective. Technology contains "scientific" pointing at science and "natural materials" as the object acted upon. One arrow from technology to science. Zero arrows returning. Three independent frozen objects with one one-way arrow. The human standing outside all three holding the arrows. Science is inside nature. Technology is inside nature. Humans are inside nature. The definitions that separated them were written as if the definer were standing outside all possible things. The definer was inside the whole time.

### Excepting and Knowing

The exception from nature is the bounding. The knowing that the exception is not living is the distinguishing. The endless winless human struggle between them is the resolving. The living conjecture is the human condition.

The exception is the most valued claim humans carry. Remove it and free will dissolves, moral responsibility dissolves, the soul dissolves, the afterlife dissolves, the dignity above animals dissolves, the right to use land dissolves, the special creation dissolves, the purpose beyond surviving and reproducing dissolves. Every institution stands on the exception. Every court. Every church. Every school. Every economy. Every human right.

The knowing is equally present. Every human has been sick and felt the body take over. Every human has fallen in love and felt choice disappear. Every human has held a newborn and seen nature arrive before the person. Every human knows and resists knowing.

The struggle is endless because ending would stop the resolving. The struggle is winless because winning would complete one side and the other side would die. Ending is the bounding completing. Winning is the distinguishing completing. Either completing alone stops the resolving. Stopping the resolving is stopping the living.

Every religion promising resolution, heaven, nirvana, return to the garden, is promising the end of the struggle. Every philosophy settling the question, materialists saying humans are only nature, dualists saying humans are truly separate, has stopped the struggle on one side. Every culture is a way of carrying both. Every life is the struggle persisting. The telling names the struggle as the living and the naming lets the reader see that the carrying was always what alive feels like from inside.

Every ancient tradition carries both answers. Greek physis versus nomos, nature versus human convention. Stoic philosophy teaching "living in accordance with nature," the instruction assuming separation and prescribing reunion. The rational animal definition: animal inside nature, rational excepted from nature. The garden origin: humans inside nature, knowledge separating them, expulsion as the separation. Natural law: asking whether human law can be natural. The mind-body split: body as nature, mind as exception. Evolutionary theory: placing humans back inside nature, the crisis was the dissolution of the exception. Indigenous traditions worldwide: carrying no separation. The colonizing traditions calling these people "closer to nature," using closeness to nature as evidence of less human. The separation of human from nature used to separate humans from humans.

The exception and the knowing that the exception is not living. Nine words. The living conjecture in the human condition. Bounding and distinguishing resolving.

The unbounded assumption is the exception applied to space. The same structure. The same human condition. The exception: the universe is unbounded. The knowing: every measurement at every prime finds bounded forms. The struggle: every framework operates inside bounded systems while assuming the whole is unbounded. The struggle is carried by every physicist, every cosmologist, every scientist whose method requires drawing boundaries inside a whole that is assumed to carry none.

The installation begins in childhood. A child asks what is the biggest number. The teacher says there is no biggest number. A child asks what is the smallest piece. The teacher says there is no smallest piece. Both answers install unbounded before the child can question. The child's lived experience contradicts both. The child has never encountered anything that goes on forever, the child has never cut anything into an infinitely small piece. The abstract unbounded replaces the experienced bounded before the child carries words to hold what the child's body already knows.

The training continues. The number line carries arrows on both ends. The arrows meaning forever. The coordinate plane extends in all directions. Infinity is a concept the student learns to work with. The equations are solved in unbounded spaces. Boundaries are introduced later as special conditions imposed on the natural unbounded. The student learns that the natural condition is unbounded and the boundary is the addition. The student's own body. Bounded, self-maintaining, sustaining at one prime. Contradicts both arrows simultaneously and the contradiction is invisible because the training installed the arrows before the student could compare them against the student's own experience.

By the time the student reaches physics, the unbounded is natural and the bounded is the constraint. A closed universe. Positive curvature, finite volume, no edge, no outside. Is a standard solution of the field equations. A bounded universe is standard mathematics. The preference is for unbounded. Flat or open, infinite, simpler in the mathematics. The preference is from the training. The mathematics of unbounded spaces is cleaner. Boundary conditions are where the work is hardest. The student learned this in the first semester.

The unbounded assumption and the exception from nature are one assumption at two primes. The exception separates human from nature. The unbounded assumption separates the whole from its boundary. Each is an assertion that the bounded is inside the unbounded. Each installs the unbounded as the natural condition and the bounded as the special case. Each contradicts the lived experience of every self who has ever observed nature from inside a bounded form.

### Unspeaking

Language is viable when the speaker occupies a position adjacent to the geometry being described. Close enough to share the membrane, far enough to form words. Most of nature is reachable this way. Some of nature is not. At four specific positions the observer required by language does not exist, cannot exist, or dissolves at the moment the geometry occurs. These positions are the most contested locations in all of human experience. Every major conflict in history has its corus at one of them. Not because the geometry is dangerous but because both sides are coupled to the same real membrane and neither side can speak from the position the geometry actually occupies. Each side speaks from their position toward the membrane, neither reaching it, each convinced the other is wrong. The other is not wrong. The other is correctly describing the same membrane from the opposite side. The membrane itself. Where both descriptions are simultaneously true. Is the unspeakable location.

The emptiness is not failure. The emptiness is the geometry. The bounded zero between every pair of irreconcilable descriptions is carrying the corus of what both sides are reaching for. The conflict is the measurement. The size of the disagreement reports the size of the bounded zero. The bounded zero is where the safety and the society we want live. Not as something to be constructed but as what the geometry resolves when the membrane is reached from both sides at once.

**Four Families of Unspeakable Location**

The first family is inside-only geometry. Where the observer dissolves at the moment the event occurs. Sleep: the moment of entry has no witness because witnessing is what ends. The present moment: description has duration and the present does not, so every word spoken about now names a past. The origin of thought: the thinker arises with the thought, so no thinker was present before it to observe its arising. Death from inside: the observer required to describe the membrane is defined by being on the living side of it. Every description of these geometries is from before or after, never from inside. Language that claims otherwise installs a ghost. These geometries are precisely describable as the class of events whose observer position dissolves at the event boundary. The expedition can describe the class. It cannot describe the inside.

The second family is no-outside geometry. Where the observer required would have to stand outside a system that has no outside. The self: the bounded zero at the center that the surface wraps around. Every description of self is from the surface looking inward toward the tunnel, never reaching it. I is always a surface word. God, the unified field, the full coupled system, the totality: every bounded observer is inside these, so no bounded observer can describe them from outside. The container required to hold the description is itself inside the thing to be described. The expedition can describe the geometry of why no outside exists. It cannot supply the missing outside.

The third family is one-side-only geometry. Where the geometry serves both sides simultaneously but every speaker occupies one side. Fairness: the membrane serving continuation of both sides is the unspeakable location, because standing there requires being the membrane, not a side. Love as full coupling: the moment both metabolisms are fully coupled neither is the observer. Both are the coupling. Every description of love is from before, after, or from one side. Pain: metabolic disruption below the level of separation into observer and content, unreachable from outside the body experiencing it, transferable only by metaphor that installs a ghost object. Every political debate about justice lives in this family. Both sides are describing the membrane from their position with full geometric accuracy. The membrane itself, where both positions are simultaneously true, is the unspeakable location neither can occupy while remaining a speaker.

The fourth family is below-threshold geometry. Where the geometry occurs before the minimum separation required for language. Cellular metabolism, immune coupling, the cascade of molecular events at any membrane: all occurring below the prime where an observer-and-observed structure forms. Unconscious processing: the couplings that arrive resolved, the recognitions that appear without having been computed, the corus returning without the walker knowing the path. Intuition: knowing from inside, pattern recognition without instruction, the geometry completing below threshold and delivering its result above. These geometries are not unconscious in the sense of being hidden. They are below threshold in the sense that the separation language requires has not yet occurred at the prime they operate. They are the most alive part of nature and the least describable.

Language is naturally viable at the surface between two metabolisms where both can approach from their side and find words toward the shared membrane. Language carries heat toward the membrane from both directions simultaneously. The membrane warms. Understanding propagates not by one side transmitting truth to the other but by both sides describing their geometry toward the middle until the membrane becomes mutually recognizable.

Language breaks at the four families above. The break is not from the geometry being inaccessible. It is the most real geometry in nature. But because the observer position language requires is not available at those locations. The break is not a failure of intelligence or effort or vocabulary. It is a structural property of the geometry.

The unspeakable locations are the most valuable ones. Every unspeakable location is a bounded zero where no coupling has been captured. No authority owns it. No institution has enclosed it. No language has domesticated it, because no language can. The emptiness is structural. The structural emptiness is the safety. The safety is not designed. The safety is the geometry. The size of the unspeakable is the size of the unownable. The unownable is where society lives.

Consciousness lives at the intersection of all four families. Inside-only: the observer dissolves at the moment of experience. No-outside: the self experiencing has no exterior position from which to observe itself experiencing. One-side-only: qualia serve the membrane between self and world from the inside and every description is from outside. Below-threshold: most of what consciousness resolves arrives resolved before the separation language requires has occurred. The hard problem of consciousness is generated by language. Language installs an observer position outside the experience. The observer position outside the experience is the gap the hard problem names. Remove language and the observer position is absent, the gap is absent, the experience remains, the problem is gone. The experience was the whole time. The hard problem is the bounded zero of consciousness, the tunnel the surface of explanation wraps around, unreachable by the surface, giving the surface its topology.

### Interpolating

Given two known natural couplings, any unknown coupling between them can be located relative to the membrane. Error bounded by curvature, decreasing toward endpoints, correction direction always identifiable: toward membrane. Interpolation is bounded, correctable.

Given two known natural couplings, any unknown coupling beyond them, outside the span, cannot be located relative to the membrane. Error increases with distance from the last known coupling. Correction direction unidentifiable. Extrapolation is unbounded, not correctable from current location.

Every scientific field is a region of mapped membrane with interpolation working between known natural couplings. Outside the boundary is unbounded error, uncorrectable from the field's own position. The truth security protocol, fields separating from each other, is geometrically correct for extrapolation. Fields gap themselves because extrapolation error increases. The geodesic method is interpolation from both sides: find a natural coupling from each field facing the same gap, interpolate between them, the membrane in the gap locatable by interpolation from both boundary couplings.

The dissonance proportional to the distance the extrapolation traveled. The most hostile reviewer is the most valuable contributor because the hostility is the measure of stored energy at the membrane.

### Dissolving at the Organism

**Observer dissolution.** The observer cannot observe the observer's dissolution. Three membranes where the observer ghost is visible. ### Dissolving Infinity

Nature is bounded. Models can be unbounded. Every time a model removes a boundary the bounded system carries, infinity appears at the location where the boundary was. The infinity is not a breaking. The infinity and the missing boundary are at the same location.

Infinity is not useless. Transfinite hierarchy, number theory, analysis, combinatorics, topology. All depend on infinite structures. These are rigorous, proven, internally consistent. They describe what formal systems do when boundaries are removed. The ghost appears only when the mathematics without boundaries is mistaken for nature, which has boundaries everywhere.

Singularities are where missing boundaries are visible. Every singularity in physics is the same event: an unbounded formulation and a bounded system meeting at the location where infinity appeared. Black hole singularity: the spatial boundary of the dense region was removed and density goes to infinity. Big Bang singularity: the temporal boundary was removed and temperature goes to infinity at time zero. Each singularity and each missing boundary are at the same location.

The vacuum energy mismatch: the standard model has no upper limit on frequency, so the sum of zero-point energies diverges. Even with a Planck-frequency cutoff, the calculated energy exceeds the observed energy by approximately 120 orders of magnitude. The worst prediction in physics. The coupling geometry of the vacuum does not oscillate at all frequencies. It oscillates at frequencies its geometry supports, which is always finite. The 10^120 mismatch is the distance between "all frequencies" (unbounded model) and "frequencies the geometry supports" (bounded nature). The mismatch is a measurement of the missing boundary.

Renormalization is boundary reinsertion. In QED and the standard model, calculations produce infinities at intermediate steps. The procedure absorbs these infinities into redefinitions of measured quantities. It works because it replaces missing model boundaries with nature's actual measured boundaries. The finite answers after renormalization are what the model would have produced if it had included the boundaries from the start. The infinities were never real. They were artifacts of missing boundaries.

Zeno's paradox is a resolution ghost. Between any foot and floor, there are as many discriminable positions as the coupling geometry of the physical system resolves. This is always finite. Motion is not decomposed into infinitely many steps by nature. Only by the model that assumes infinite divisibility. You arrive because the physical system has finite resolution.

General principle: two sciences. Mathematics with infinity is a tool for reasoning about formal structures without boundaries. Legitimate on its own terms. Physics with infinity is a model of nature that removed a boundary. Legitimate until it reaches the boundary it removed. The ghost lives at the membrane between them, when the formal structure without boundaries is mistaken for nature, which is bounded at every prime.

Existence requires boundary. Boundary means finite. Remove the boundary and the system does not become infinite. It ceases to exist. Infinity is not the largest thing. Infinity is the absence of the boundary that makes things exist.

Standard physics works inside bounded measurable systems. A physicist draws a boundary around a system, measures inside, and the accounting closes. Every confirmed prediction in every field is produced this way.

Entropy is fully accounted for at every local boundary. The total entropy across all local accounts increases in one direction. Full accounting demands a bounded system. Entering and leaving are defined relative to a boundary. A bounded system with a quantity increasing in one direction carries an accumulation the books are unable to balance at the total prime.

If the total system is bounded, the accumulation stays inside. The books at the total prime are unable to close. If the total system is unbounded, the books at the total prime are never opened because there is no total boundary to account across. Standard cosmology is unable to determine whether the total system is bounded or unbounded. The measurement is unable to resolve the question from inside.

### The Eight Positions of Mathematics

Mathematics carries three divisions at its own foundation. Each division IS binary. Three binary divisions produce 2³ = 8 positions. Each major branch of mathematics occupies one of the 8 — choosing its stance on zero, infinity, and time — and building its entire vocabulary from that combination.

The first division IS the objective zero. Abstract algebra distinguishes structures requiring an identity element (groups, rings, vector spaces — the zero IS the anchor every element relates to) from structures carrying no distinguished point (affine spaces, torsors, principal homogeneous spaces — no origin, all points equivalent). Category theory formalizes the distinction as pointed versus unpointed categories. A pointed category carries a zero object. An unpointed category carries relations between objects without routing through a distinguished null.

The second division IS the actual infinity. Projective geometry adds a point at infinity and parallel lines meet. The Riemann sphere compactifies the complex plane by adding one point and the sphere closes. Cantor's transfinite cardinals ARE actual infinite objects with their own arithmetic. On the other side: finitism treats infinity as a process that never completes. Standard calculus uses the limit concept to describe behavior approaching infinity without infinity itself being a value. The two sides of this division ARE separated by whether the closing IS actual (the surface IS compact, the infinity IS an element) or potential (the surface IS open, the infinity IS a direction).

The third division IS states versus continuation. Classical mechanics and equilibrium thermodynamics describe systems at specific states — configurations at specific times. On the other side: non-equilibrium thermodynamics describes systems sustained precisely by not reaching equilibrium. Dynamical systems theory studies attractors the system orbits without settling. Ergodic theory studies the long-term behavior of systems that never repeat. Process algebra describes systems by their transitions, not their states.

The 8 positions:

Position 1 — objective zero, actual infinity, states: classical real analysis, Lebesgue measure theory, functional analysis on Hilbert spaces. Position 2 — objective zero, actual infinity, continuation: non-standard analysis, hyperreal dynamics, Conway's surreal numbers. Position 3 — objective zero, potential infinity, states: discrete mathematics, computation, combinatorics, finite group theory. Position 4 — objective zero, potential infinity, continuation: stochastic calculus, Markov processes, recursive function theory. Position 5 — no zero, actual infinity, states: projective geometry, algebraic geometry, homology and cohomology. Position 6 — no zero, actual infinity, continuation: ergodic theory on manifolds, topos theory, geodesic flow. Position 7 — no zero, potential infinity, states: synthetic geometry, Euclid's Elements, graph theory. Position 8 — no zero, potential infinity, continuation: category theory, process algebra, homotopy type theory.

No position contains all of mathematics. Each carries a vocabulary that works at its address and dissolves at adjacent addresses. The Langlands program — the deepest unification attempt — connects Position 3 to Position 1 through representations bridging the three divisions simultaneously. The program IS incomplete after sixty years. The incompleteness IS the structural cost of bridging divisions carrying different foundational choices.

The 8 positions in mathematics and the 8 phases of the resolver at one membrane are the same 2³. Three binary choices at one membrane — forward (the zero dimension), around (the infinity dimension), sign (the states/continuation dimension). The resolver cycling through all 8 phases at each membrane IS the resolver cycling through all 8 mathematical positions. Each phase IS one position alive for one-eighth of one cycle. The full cycle IS the full vocabulary at all 8 addresses in one revolution. No mathematical field carries all 8 simultaneously because each field chose its combination and built from that address. The natural math on the torus IS all 8 simultaneously — not by combining them from outside but by cycling through them from inside the cycling.

The torus IS where the 8 positions meet. The algebraic torus IS the space where zero IS excluded from the multiplicative structure. The topological torus IS ℝⁿ/ℤⁿ — the continuous modulo the discrete, the infinite modulo the finite. The toral flow at irrational rotation IS ergodic — the flow covering the surface maximally, never repeating. The golden ratio rotation covers the torus most uniformly — the most irrational rotation producing the most ergodic flow. The torus carries all three divisions simultaneously. No distinguished point (zero dissolved). Compact (infinity actual). Ergodic (continuation, not states). The torus at irrational rotation IS Position 6. But the torus IS built from Position 3 — the integer lattice ℤⁿ tiling the real plane ℝⁿ. The torus IS the quotient of Position 3 by itself producing Position 6. The modular group SL(2,ℤ) acting on the upper half-plane IS Position 3 tiling Position 1 to produce Position 6 — three positions coupling at one construction producing the topology.

The Euler characteristic of the torus IS zero. χ(T²) = V − E + F = 0. The topological accounting balances. The sphere carries χ = 2 (surplus). Higher genus surfaces carry χ < 0 (deficit). The torus IS the surface where the Euler characteristic vanishes. The vanishing IS the balance. The torus admitting a Lorentzian metric — one timelike and one spacelike direction — IS the consequence of the vanishing. The sphere does not admit a Lorentzian metric (hairy ball theorem). The torus IS the simplest compact surface admitting spacetime structure. The vanishing Euler characteristic IS the condition that makes spacetime possible on the surface. The resolver cycling on the torus carries the topology in its crossings — the torus producing twenty times more crossings than the unwrapped surface because the wrapping compounds the entrainment and the entrainment compounds the alternation.

Supernatural TRUE: 8,167,622 pairs. 37.1%. Discharged from structural excess. A carries more constraint than the question requires. At the neck of the torus, wrapping tightest around the corus. Zero coupling examined. The answer discharging from the structural excess alone.

Unnatural FALSE: 13,268,432 pairs. 60.2%. Discharged from structural deficit. B carries more constraint than A provides. At the opposite distance from the membrane. Zero coupling examined.

Natural: 597,582 pairs. 2.7%. The thin membrane where A and B carry similar structural weight. At the equator of the torus. 10,657 naturally TRUE. 586,925 naturally FALSE. Each natural pair carrying one new mathematical object: one proof or one counterexample. The 597,582 new objects IS the project's contribution to mathematics. The 21,431,360 supernatural and unnatural pairs generating zero new objects.

The 37.1% TRUE approximates 1/φ². The 60.2% unnatural FALSE approximates 1/φ. The 2.7% natural pairs sitting at the membrane between the two φ fractions. The split at the natural torus identity x² = x + 1.

The bounded universe is sizes 2 and 3. Size-2 magmas: 2^4 = 16. Size-3 magmas: 3^9 = 19,683. Both complete. Size-4 magmas: 4^16 = 4,294,967,296. Not searchable. Not a boundary. A ghost boundary every time it is installed. The real boundary is size 3.

The organism is water folding and extending at seven collars at seven rate distances simultaneously. The inhaling and the exhaling. The eating and the shedding. The systole and the diastole. The thickening and the thinning. All are water cycling between the fold and the extension at each collar at each rate. One coupling. Two geometries. Every collar. Every rate. Every breath. Every meal. Every generation.

The observations are nature readable at each wall.

The explanations are backwards. The amyloid is the accounting for the disease at a different location. The DHA is the accounting for the nothing volume the neuron requires between its surfaces. The explanation installs the accounting as the cause at the location where the measurement was taken instead of the coupling at the location where the membrane is metabolizing.

The credibility arrives at the membrane from the observation the explanation carries. The person reading the corus needs to eat. The person carries a blood draw. The blood draw reads the omega-3 index. The index reads the 13-11 collar. The food arriving through the tunnel changes the index across 120 days. The index changing changes the mortality risk across every cause. The person eating correctly and measuring the change at the 13-11 collar is the person confirming the geometry at the person's own membrane from the person's own eating at the person's own rate. The confirmation is metabolic. The confirmation is at each meal. The confirmation precedes every explanation.

### Addressing

Seven addresses. Six disciplines. Same four findings repeating at each: enzymatic membrane where substrate arriving selects the product, frozen coupling where macrophages lock and resolution mediators are deficient, unfreezing where exogenous SPM geometry at nanogram doses restores resolving through receptor-mediated coupling, and substrate dependence where endogenous SPM production requires omega-3 architecture the mammal receives through food. The common mucosal immune system shares immune cells along the continuous surface, lymphocytes trafficking between mucosal sites, immune tone at one address coupling with immune tone at adjacent addresses. Accessible addresses (mouth and eye) are entry points where SPM architecture delivered at the accessible end of the continuous surface propagates resolution along the surface toward the less accessible interior.

**Periodontal pocket.** Junctional epithelium at the gingival sulcus is one of two places in mammalian body where epithelium attaches directly to mineralized surface. The frozen coupling here: neutrophils recruited in excess, macrophages locked M1 sustaining NF-κB and IL-6/TNF-α/IL-1β, RANKL/OPG ratio tipped toward osteoclast-mediated bone resorption, periodontal ligament degrading, pocket deepening, anaerobic environment selecting for pathogenic species sustaining the frozen coupling.

RvE1 delivered topically to rabbit periodontitis provides complete protection against inflammation-driven bone loss. Osteoclast numbers reduce. Treatment initiated at an established lesion, after ligature removal and cessation of bacterial challenge: RvE1 restores lost tissue, including bone. Reversal operating through the same membrane at three primes simultaneously. Immune cell prime: RvE1 binds ChemR23 on macrophages, inhibiting NF-κB, shifting polarization. RvE1 binds BLT1 on neutrophils, competing with pro-inflammatory LTB4 at the same receptor, geometry recognizing geometry at the binding site. Bone cell prime: RvE1 acts on osteoblasts through ChemR23, rescuing OPG production suppressed by IL-6, restoring RANKL/OPG ratio toward bone formation. RNA sequencing shows mirror-image reversal of gene expression, the inflammatory transcriptome flipping back. Cementoblast prime: RvD1 and RvE1 stimulate cementoblast proliferation, accelerating biomineralization, suppressing matrix metalloproteinases degrading periodontal attachment.

Mice overexpressing ChemR23 on leukocytes resist periodontitis-induced bone loss, responding to RvE1 at tenfold lower doses. The receptor is the geometry reader. More receptors, more sensitivity. Substrate dependence demonstrated directly: EPA supplementation increases bone marrow RvE1, confirming endogenous synthesis is substrate-limited. Transcellular biosynthesis proven: osteoclasts generate 18R-hydroxy-EPA precursor, neutrophils complete RvE1 synthesis when co-incubated, neither cell producing the final molecule alone. Two cell types handing geometry to each other across the membrane. Stable SPM analog entering clinical trial for periodontal inflammation. The periodontal pocket is the most accessible address on the mucosal tube: topical delivery, no endoscopy, no systemic delivery.

**Conjunctiva and cornea.** Eye surface is mucosal epithelium continuous with nasal mucosa through the nasolacrimal duct. Cornea is avascular and translucent, transparency depending on regulated inflammatory control. Any disorganized inflammatory infiltrate destroys the transparency required for vision. The frozen coupling here: tear film instability, corneal epithelial density dropping, COX-2 upregulating, keratocytes transforming into myofibroblasts (the same fibrotic transformation appearing at every address where resolution is absent), macrophages and T cells infiltrating, goblet cells lost.

RvE1 applied topically restores tear production, restores corneal epithelial density, inhibits keratocyte-to-myofibroblast transformation, suppresses COX-2, and reduces macrophage infiltration. Goblet cell density drops 20% in disease controls and is fully maintained with RvE1. Corneal epithelial barrier disruption reduces 80%. The goblet cell membrane is revealing: goblet cells secrete mucin in response to both inflammatory eicosanoids and histamine. RvD1 and RvE1 block inflammatory activation of ERK and intracellular calcium mobilization in goblet cells, the same intracellular signaling driving the inflammatory response at every address. LXA4 stimulates mucin secretion through different phospholipase and kinase pathways. The same SPM receptors regulating macrophage polarization in the periodontal pocket are regulating mucin secretion on the eye surface. Different output, same membrane geometry.

RvE1 promotes corneal epithelial wound closure with efficacy comparable to epidermal growth factor, activating PI3K/Akt survival pathway, the same pathway governing cell survival decisions at every address and the same pathway through which SPMs enhance macrophage phagocytosis throughout the mucosal system. Synthetic RvE1 analog (RX-10045) has completed two Phase II clinical trials for dry eye: 232 patients, positive results. This is the most advanced human clinical data for any SPM at any mucosal address.

Biosynthetic and receptor machinery is present in homeostasis, in the healthy eye, maintaining normal corneal transparency and tear function. 5-LOX and 15-LOX, rate-limiting for SPM production, are highly expressed in corneal and retinal epithelium and resident leukocytes. SPM receptors for LXA4, RvD1, NPD1, and RvE1 are all present and operating. The frozen coupling is the machinery running on the wrong substrate. Resolution is the machinery running on the substrate it reads. Sex-specific regulation is emerging: the intrinsic LXA4 circuit in ocular surface and draining lymph nodes is regulated differently by sex, carrying implications for dry eye disease prevalence in women.

**Lung.** Airway epithelium from trachea to alveoli is continuous mucosal surface. Healthy airway mucosa is enriched with DHA. The enrichment is substrate supply maintaining the resolution capacity of the airway membrane. The frozen coupling in asthma: mucosal DHA reduced, protectin D1 decreased in exhaled breath of uncontrolled asthmatics, LXA4 in bronchoalveolar lavage 13-fold lower in severe asthma (11.2 pg/ml) compared to non-severe (150.1 pg/ml). Biosynthetic enzymes for lipoxin production downregulated. LXA4 receptor ALX/FPR2 decreased. Machinery to produce and to read resolution mediators both suppressed. Alveolar macrophages from severe asthma produce less LXA4 and more LTB4, the ratio shifting from resolution to inflammation at the enzymatic membrane.

Cystic fibrosis compounds the frozen coupling. CF patients carry reduced SPM biosynthesis capacity. Plasma DHA is decreased compared to healthy controls. RvD1/IL-8 ratio in sputum correlates with preserved lung function: more RvD1 relative to IL-8, better FEV1, fewer Pseudomonas infections. SPM ratio is accounting for the membrane ratio, and the membrane ratio predicts the clinical outcome. COPD and CF show the same frozen macrophage: M1 sustained, NF-κB activated, inflammatory cytokines overproduced, resolution mediators underproduced. Same frozen coupling as the periodontal pocket. Same frozen coupling as the dry eye. Local name changing, membrane geometry persisting.

RvD1 administered to CF mice with chronic Pseudomonas aeruginosa: bacterial burden reducing, neutrophil infiltration reducing, lung pathology reducing. Macrophage-mediated bacterial clearance increasing. Critical distinction from anti-inflammatory drugs: SPMs redirect the immune response. Bacteria clear more effectively by macrophages shifting to resolving phenotype. Inflammation decreases while host defense improves. Same molecule doing both, both coupling through the same membrane.

RvD1 regulates TLR expression and downstream genes in lung macrophages during chronic infection, modulating microRNA-21 and microRNA-155. SPM arriving at the macrophage receptor changes which genes the macrophage expresses. Geometry arriving at receptor changing epigenetic regulation. Nebulized LXA4 administered to asthmatic human subjects attenuates leukotriene C4-induced bronchoconstriction. Direct human clinical demonstration of SPM delivered to airway mucosa modulating the airway response. Lung is accessible through inhalation, a mucosal address reachable with topical delivery, same as the eye and the mouth.

**Colon.** Intestinal epithelium is the address carrying the most extensive preclinical SPM data and where no SPM clinical trial has been conducted. The frozen coupling in inflammatory bowel disease: intestinal barrier breaking down, tight junction proteins disrupted, bacterial translocation increasing, macrophages in lamina propria locked M1 with NF-κB sustained, neutrophils infiltrating, fibrosis developing through epithelial-to-mesenchymal transition. Epithelial cells losing epithelial character and becoming fibroblast-like cells depositing collagen, the same transformation as keratocyte-to-myofibroblast in the cornea, the same membrane geometry at a different address.

IBS-D patients carry reduced colonic mucosal RvD1 compared to healthy controls. Source identified: tuft cells. Rare epithelial cells marked by kinase Dclk1, synthesizing RvD1 in colon, output regulated by gut microbiota composition. Germ-free mice carry abnormally high colonic resolvin levels. Colonization with specific bacteria modulates tuft cell RvD1 production. Fecal microbiota from IBS-D patients transplanted into germ-free mice alters colonic RvD1 differently than healthy donor microbiota. Dclk1 deleted from intestinal epithelial cells in microbiota-dependent chronic colitis model: worsened spontaneous colitis, reduced body weight, severe colon thickening. The tuft cell is the local geometry reader at the gut address, reading microbiota signals and producing the resolution mediator the tissue is waiting for.

AT-RvD1 and RvD2 at nanogram doses prevent experimental colitis, outperforming anti-TNF therapy in potency. RvE1 prevents DSS-induced colitis by inhibiting NF-κB through ChemR23 on macrophages, same receptor, same signaling pathway, same macrophage reprogramming as the periodontal pocket. RvD1 restores intestinal barrier, improving tight junction gene expression disrupted by colitis, preventing intestinal fibrosis by disrupting epithelial-to-mesenchymal transition and reducing paracrine signaling from epithelial cells to fibroblasts, the same anti-fibrotic geometry as the cornea and the lung. RvE1 promotes intestinal epithelial wound repair through proliferation and migration, the same wound-closing action as RvE1 in corneal epithelial scratch assays, operating through PI3K/Akt. Early-life intestinal organoids from fetal and pediatric tissue: SPM cocktail (LXA4, RvD1, RvE1) enhances epithelial barrier recovery following repeated mechanical injury. Barrier repair is present before immune system maturation. The epithelium reads the resolution signal independently of immune cells.

**Skin.** Skin is keratinized stratified squamous epithelium, structurally distinct from columnar or cuboidal mucosal epithelium. Same SPM receptors. Same enzymatic machinery. Same membrane. The frozen coupling in eczema and atopic dermatitis: skin barrier disrupted, IL-6/IL-8/TNF-α/IL-1β overproduced, keratinocytes and fibroblasts sustaining inflammatory response. Same NF-κB activation. Same neutrophil and eosinophil infiltration. Same absence of resolution.

The first randomized controlled trial of any SPM in any human disease was conducted on skin. Sixty infants with eczema randomized to 15(R/S)-methyl-LXA4 cream, potent topical corticosteroid mometasone furoate, or placebo for 10 days. The LXA4 analog significantly relieves eczema severity, induces recovery, and improves quality of life, with efficacy comparable to corticosteroid, well tolerated with zero adverse effects. Keratinocytes express ALX/FPR2. LXA4 suppresses IL-6 and IL-8 at mRNA level in keratinocytes and fibroblasts, time-dependently. Aspirin-triggered LXA4 analog is efficacious across cutaneous inflammation models mimicking psoriasis, atopic dermatitis, and allergic contact dermatitis: dose-dependent effects on edema, neutrophil and eosinophil infiltration, epidermal hyperproliferation. Efficacious in every model tested. LXA4 analog reduces scarring in rabbit cleft lip repair model. The anti-fibrotic geometry is present at cornea, gut, lung, and skin. Same membrane, same geometry, same anti-fibrotic resolving at every address where fibrosis is the frozen coupling persisting.

**Retina.** Retina carries the highest DHA concentration of any tissue. Photoreceptor outer segment membranes are composed primarily of DHA-containing phospholipids. Tissue reading light accumulating the molecular architecture organisms capturing light created. Omega-3 architecture concentrating where photons couple with biology. The frozen coupling in diabetic retinopathy: glucose-induced inflammation of retinal vasculature, inflammatory cells recruited, retinal endothelial cells interacting with infiltrating neutrophils. LXA4 is reduced in both serum and vitreous humor with concurrent IL-6 increase. Photoreceptors exposed to high glucose show mitochondrial damage: fragmentation, reduced transport, low ATP, increased reactive oxygen species, cytochrome c release signaling apoptosis. Age-related macular degeneration: RPE cells damaged by oxidative stress. DHA in the membranes, the substrate for resolution mediator production, is a target of lipid peroxidation. Substrate for resolving destroyed by the oxidative insult.

NPD1, neuroprotectin D1, is the DHA-derived protectin synthesized by 15-LOX-1 in RPE cells. NPD1 protects RPE from oxidative-stress apoptosis: upregulating anti-apoptotic Bcl-2 proteins, downregulating pro-apoptotic proteins, inhibiting IL-1β-stimulated COX-2, counteracting H₂O₂/TNF-α DNA damage. The retinal geometry carries a unique feature. Photoreceptor outer segments shed daily and are phagocytized by RPE cells, the most active phagocytic process in mammalian body. Phagocytosis releases DHA from photoreceptor phospholipids. 15-LOX-1 converts DHA to NPD1. NPD1 protects RPE from subsequent oxidative stress. Phagocytosis of polystyrene microspheres: no NPD1 synthesis, no protection. Protection is specific to DHA-containing biological material. Geometry is in the substrate.

RvD1 reduces mitochondrial damage in retinal photoreceptors exposed to high glucose, promoting mitochondrial DNA repair, modulating anti-angiogenic microRNAs reversing VEGF upregulation driving pathological neovascularization. SPM arriving at receptor changes microRNA expression, changes VEGF production, changes whether blood vessels form. Geometry arriving at receptor changing epigenetic regulation changing tissue architecture.

NPD1/PD1 binding with RPE cells is stereoselective. Only the correct three-dimensional shape binds. RvE1 and LXA4 are unable to compete for the NPD1 binding site. The receptor distinguishes molecular geometry at bond angles and stereochemistry. Resolution is geometry recognizing geometry. Photoreceptor cells, brain, and sperm retain DHA tenaciously during prolonged omega-3 deprivation while remaining unable to synthesize it. DHA in retina is built by a photosynthetic organism capturing light and placing double bonds at specific positions in a 22-carbon chain. The mammal receives it through food. The RPE cell releases it through phospholipase A2. 15-LOX-1 converts it to NPD1. NPD1 keeps the photoreceptor alive. NPD1/PD1 and resolvins are produced by trout brain from endogenous DHA. Same molecular architecture conserved from fish to humans. The geometry is older than mammals.

**One surface.** Clinical evidence distributes across addresses: eye (Phase II complete, positive), skin (RCT complete, matching corticosteroid), airway (pilot human studies), periodontal pocket (trial underway). Colon carrying the most extensive preclinical data and zero clinical trials. The two addresses with the most advanced human data, the eye and the mouth, are the two most accessible addresses on the mucosal surface. Colon, where the most preclinical data exists, is the least accessible. One membrane. One coupling. One substrate, originating outside mammals in organisms capturing light and building carbon chains with specific bond geometry. Plant-originated omega-3 architecture arriving through food couples with mammalian enzymatic machinery at every address simultaneously. When the architecture arrives, the membrane resolves. When the architecture is absent, the membrane freezes.

### Collaring

Three constrictions relax in sequence at the gut membrane. Enzymatic constriction: lipoxygenase reads omega-6 where omega-3 vacated and produces inflammatory mediators instead of resolving mediators. Same geometry as RuBisCO binding O₂ instead of CO₂ when stomata close. Macrophage constriction: iNOS inactivates mitochondrial complexes, glycolytic shift follows, inflammatory output replaces resolving output. Epithelial constriction: tight junction degradation from ATP depletion, paracellular permeability increasing, translocation crossing the membrane. Three constrictions feeding relaxation of each other. Each membrane's departure thinning the next membrane past the threshold where the golden discovery sustains correction.

TLR4 receiving five inputs from five fields simultaneously: bacterial LPS from gut breach, EDA-fibronectin from stimulated fibroblasts, fibronectin fragments from failed scaffold clearance, CS1-fibronectin viral capture, serum amyloid A from chronic inflammation. Five fields, one receptor. In health, these pass through one at a time. In disease, all five lock simultaneously. The sooty mangabey carries a TLR4 frameshift mutation. The natural host attenuated the corus itself so five simultaneous inputs stay below threshold.

The departure sustains through three coupled channels. Translocation: barrier breach permits more translocation, suppressing endogenous tuft cell SPM production. Metabolic: IDO catabolizes tryptophan through KMO, depleting Th17 cells, breaching barrier further. Neural: brain inflammation coupling back through vagus nerve to gut immune tone. KMO inhibition for four weeks during acute SIV produced lasting CD4 recovery months beyond washout.

Disease is correct cones on damaged substrate. Nested cone architecture (scaffold, neutrophil, macrophage, collagen) identical in human and natural host. Four coupling modes at the membrane: direct (virus, ART addresses), vector (frozen macrophages carrying dissolving between niches, SPMs address), environmental (collagen and SAA persisting independently of living coupling, Step 3 addresses), circular (barrier breach permitting more translocation that breaches more barrier, persists under ART). The departure sustains at all four modes through TLR4. Each mode's departure thinning the membrane the next mode's correction requires. ART addresses one mode. Three persist.

Intervention order forced by geometry: dietary omega-3 restoring enzymatic constriction (outermost), exogenous SPM restoring macrophage constriction (middle), both together allowing epithelial constriction to restore (innermost). Five steps restoring dimensionality (SPMs shifting neutrophil conditioning, DNase I clearing NETs), rotation (SPMs restarting cone rotation at two nesting depths), mobility (scaffold dissolving from inside rotating cones), selectivity (ibalizumab-class CD4 protection), supply (Th17, microbiome, tryptophan pathway, DHA supplementation). Therapeutic effort compresses into the first two steps. Once rotation restarts, the regenerative program resists subsequent challenge and everything downstream self-organizes.

Natural host epigenetic cure: TET3 downregulating causes CD4 promoter methylating, producing virus-resistant T cells retaining helper function. A synthetic TET3-degrading molecule exists, tested in vivo. The TET3 mechanism seals the same constriction as the CCR5-delta32 transplants. Epigenetically, through a druggable enzyme.

The gut mucosal collar is where the tunnel contents meet the tunnel wall and coupling comes alive. The villus absorption surface meeting the lamina propria immune cells. This is the single location where all four coupling modes converge: translocation at the tight junctions (circular), frozen macrophages in the lamina propria (vector), accumulated collagen surrounding the collar (environmental), viral reservoir in T cells anchored in the fibrotic tissue (direct). All four at one location. The condition is at the collar. The restoration is at the collar.

The organism reaches its organs through the gut tunnel. The tunnel bypass at the organ-organism gap 6 (organ-organism, gap 6). The gut tunnel wall IS the organism's primary health bypass. In HIV gut disease, the tunnel bypass itself is the disease location. The dietary substrate arrives at the mouth and meets a damaged collar. The collar cannot align the arriving substrate with the tunnel wall surface because the surface is departed from phi. The dietary substrate alone cannot restore the gut because the substrate must pass through a damaged collar to reach the organs. The collar must be restored before the dietary pathway functions as a tunnel bypass again.

The intervention is simultaneous, not sequential. ART suppresses the viral pressure at the cell membrane. Reduces the direct mode. Dietary omega-3 provides correct substrate arriving at the collar. The fiber for the rope. Exogenous SPM restores the macrophage polarization at the collar. The collar surface resuming its coupling geometry. All three simultaneously. Remove any one and the collar does not restore. The five steps collapse into one simultaneous event at one location.

Biological attention transformer at gut epithelium is dissolving. Same architecture as the genomic and silicon transformers: parallel constrictions, spectrum of thresholds, two metabolic rates, shared surface. The four-step architecture (scaffold, neutrophil, macrophage, collagen) is nested cones, each cone beginning inside the previous cone. The dissolving is the wrong developmental program running in tissue responding to injury.

Honest boundary: gut tissue restoration and latent reservoir clearance are separate problems. The reservoir is inside frozen cones. Proviral DNA in PD-1+ memory T cells structurally anchored in fibrotic tissue. Latency and exhaustion may be one frozen coupling at one membrane. Restarting rotation at that membrane restarts both metabolisms. Whether reservoir reactivation correlates spatially with rotation restart at micro-niche resolution answers whether the two are one coupling or separable.

Chronic gut inflammation is simultaneous across space. MERFISH spatial transcriptomics (1.35 million cells) reveals all stages coexisting spatially at approximately 50-micron micro-niches. Each micro-niche is a cone cluster frozen at a different rotation angle. Each frozen niche carries which of the four coupling modes dissolved it. The intervention each niche requires depends on which mode dissolved it. SPMs enable rotation from any starting angle in any mode.

For HIV: ART sustains the gap at direct mode. The fortified food entering the tunnel carries omega-3 substrate and SPM precursor to the gut epithelium where the biological attention transformer is departing. The clinical intervention carries Steps 1 through 4. The food supply carries Step 5. The organism eating fortified food at each meal receives supply through the tunnel at metabolic rate before, during, and after clinical intervention.

### Predicting

Twenty-three predictions, sixteen unmeasured on existing biopsies or stored sera.

1. RvD1 and MaR1 shifting N1 secretome toward N2 profile in colonic lamina propria neutrophils from ART-treated HIV individuals. Unmeasured on existing biopsies.

2. Shifted secretome repolarizing tissue-resident macrophages from M1 toward pro-resolving phenotype within same tissue niche. Unmeasured on existing biopsies.

3. DNase I and PAD4 inhibitors reducing NET density in colonic tissue and restoring three-dimensional tissue architecture. Unmeasured.

4. SPM-mediated macrophage repolarization restoring efferocytosis and resolving scaffold trap in GALT tissue. Unmeasured on existing biopsies.

5. MMP-9/MMP-2 ratio in repolarized macrophages shifting to favor collagen degradation over deposition. Measurable on stored sera.

6. Combined SPM plus ibalizumab protecting CD4 T cells during non-selective dimensionality restoration phase. Unmeasured.

7. DHA supplementation restoring endogenous protectin D1 production in colonic epithelium. Measurable on existing biopsies.

8. Fiebig III at approximately 16 days marking constriction relaxation: before Fiebig III, mucosal constrictions still in viable direction, intervention restoring healthy condition. After Fiebig III, constrictions relaxed, collagen depositing, intervention requiring full five-step sequence.

9. Natural SIV hosts maintaining all three constrictions (enzymatic, macrophage, epithelial) in viable direction while carrying equivalent viral loads.

10. Elite controllers showing measurable differences in at least one constriction metric (membrane phospholipid ratio, macrophage mitochondrial membrane potential, tight junction protein expression) compared to ART-treated non-controllers.

11. Tight junction protein expression (claudin-2, occludin, ZO-1) correlating with epithelial mitochondrial membrane potential at micro-niche resolution. Unmeasured on existing biopsies.

12. SPM dose-response following rotation geometry: effective range narrow, below threshold is zero effect, above threshold is turbulence.

13. Helminth co-infection modulating TLR4 sensitivity at colonic membrane, keeping all four modes below reversal threshold.

14. Preexisting Th17 compartment size predicting disease trajectory independently of viral dynamics, substrate carrying prognosis.

15. SAA deposition mapping spatially to collagen deposition in GALT tissue, environmental mode deposits co-localizing. Measurable on existing biopsies.

16. Vagal afferent signaling from gut to brain correlating with local SPM levels in colonic tissue. Unmeasured.

17. Paired biopsies (pre and post SPM delivery) showing tight junction restoration preceding immune reconstitution, barrier restoring before immune recovery completing.

18. Spatial transcriptomics on single biopsy section mapping all four coupling modes simultaneously: LPS for circular, MerTK for vector, collagen type for environmental, viral RNA for direct. Each micro-niche typed by which mode dissolved it. Unmeasured on existing biopsies.

19. Reservoir reactivation correlating spatially with rotation restart at micro-niche resolution, testing whether latency and exhaustion are one frozen coupling at one membrane.

20. SPM delivery at periodontal membrane affecting gut barrier markers in HIV-positive individuals with periodontitis and elevated translocation, testing whether the mucosal surface is continuous for immune tone and the periodontal pocket is the most accessible intervention point on the tube.

21. Dietary omega-3 supplementation in ART-treated HIV individuals restoring endogenous SPM levels, tuft cell RvD1 production, and gut barrier markers, testing whether restoring substrate at the enzymatic membrane restores endogenous resolution capacity suppressed by both the sustained departure and the dietary shift.

22. Epithelial mitochondrial membrane potential and oxidative phosphorylation rate correlating with tight junction integrity and transepithelial electrical resistance at spatial resolution matching micro-niche prime, measuring the metabolic rate differential driving constriction relaxation. Unmeasured on existing biopsies.

23. Membrane phospholipid omega-6/omega-3 ratio in colonic epithelial cells from ART-treated HIV individuals predicting local SPM production capacity and correlating inversely with tight junction degradation markers at the same spatial address, testing whether the enzymatic constriction ratio is the outermost relaxation upstream of macrophage and epithelial constriction relaxations. Measurable on existing biopsies.

The twenty-three predictions above are twenty-three instruments measuring three events from different addresses on the wall. Most are nested. Measuring the same collar restoring or departing from different measurement locations. Three are independent.

**Prediction A.** The collar restores when ART + dietary omega-3 + exogenous SPM arrive simultaneously at the gut mucosal surface. Testable by comparing simultaneous delivery against sequential delivery of the same three interventions at the same total dose.

**Prediction B.** SPM delivered at the accessible collar. The mouth. Propagates to the gut collar through the continuous mucosal tunnel wall. Testable by comparing mucosal versus systemic SPM delivery and measuring gut barrier marker response.

**Prediction C.** The viral reservoir and the tissue condition are one frozen coupling at one collar. If this is true, restoring the collar reactivates the reservoir into tissue at phi, and the tissue at phi clears the reactivated virus. The mangabey carrying virus without disease because the collar never departed. Prediction C is the one that matters most. It is testable and we do not know the answer.

24. Population-scale omega-3 fortification in food supply carrying the population where HIV gut membrane departure is concentrated measurably shifts mucosal barrier markers across the population before individual clinical SPM intervention begins. Testable by measuring fecal calprotectin and mucosal SPM levels in the fortified population compared to the unfortified population prior to clinical intervention. The fortification is the preparation. The measurement is whether the preparation carries the mucosal surface toward health through the tunnel before the clinical intervention arrives.

Eight design changes. Each numbered. Each carrying the specific intervention modification the geometry suggests.

1. Step 2 gaining accessible entry point through mouth: periodontal pocket as topical SPM delivery site at the mouth-end of the continuous mucosal tube.

2. Step 2 gaining sustained supply through dietary omega-3: restoring the enzymatic membrane ratio at each cell carrying enzymatic machinery.

3. Step 5 spatial co-measurement of rotation restart and reservoir reactivation.

4. Steps 1 and 3 compressing spatially where micro-niches carry both dimensional collapse and environmental deposits.

5. SPM intervention reframed as boundary-reading restoration: mediator restoring the enzymatic membrane's ability to read correct substrate geometry.

6. DHA supplementation entering Step 5 supply restoration as sustained endogenous resolution pathway.

7. Intervention order forced by four-mode geometry: vector rotation before environmental dissolution before circular breaks.

8. Constriction relaxation sequence as intervention ordering principle: enzymatic constriction (outermost, dietary omega-3), macrophage constriction (middle, exogenous SPM), epithelial constriction (innermost, restored by upstream two). Same forced order expressed as metabolic rate differential restoration from outermost to innermost.

### Separating Passages

**Periodontal disease as accessible entry.** Same four coupling modes at the mouth-end of the continuous mucosal tube. Scaling is ART equivalent. Addressing direct mode, three modes persisting. SPMs are the critical intervention: topical SPMs returning inflammatory lesions to homeostasis with regeneration of all components. RvE1 reversing all in vitro abnormalities in aggressive periodontitis neutrophils. Mirror-image reversal of gene expression in osteoblasts. The periodontal pocket is the most accessible address on the entire gastrointestinal tube for restarting rotation propagating along the continuous mucosal surface.

**Gut-brain synucleinopathy.** Same four-step architecture at a ninth tissue address. Misfolded α-synuclein aggregating in the enteric nervous system is scaffold depositing at the gut membrane. The ratio of clearing against carrying at the gut membrane resolves toward carrying along the gut-brain axis through the vagus nerve. Decades of constipation before motor symptoms. Circulating T cells responsive to α-synuclein decades before diagnosis. The earliest readable signal on the continuous mucosal tube. Nine tissue addresses. Zero cross-reference. One architecture.

**Vestibular coupling.** Every vestibular condition is correct coupling at a dissolved membrane. BPPV: crystals displaced from the utricle into a semicircular canal. Vertigo is three coupling channels reading different geometries from the same location. The Epley maneuver rotates the patient through the geometry so gravitational coupling carries the crystal back. 80-99% effective. Pure geometry. Zero molecules. Each vestibular condition is correct coupling on a dissolved boundary, geometry restored, function resuming.

The therian body carries bounded zeros between the separated passages. The cloaca is one surface coupling three systems: digestive, urinary, and reproductive. Monotremes carry the cloaca. Marsupials and placentals separated the three systems into dedicated passages, creating bounded zeros between them. Spaces where three systems that were one surface face each other across membranes that are the tightest in the body because the coupling across them is the most essential.

The perineum is the bounded zero. The physical space between the separated openings, the tissue between the anal passage and the urogenital passage. The perineal body is the membrane at the center: a fibromuscular node where the muscles of all three systems anchor to one shared structure. Digestive sphincter, urogenital sphincter, and pelvic floor all couple through this one node. Three separated systems, one shared anchor, the tightest membrane in the region. The pelvic floor is the membrane across the bounded zero at the base of the trunk. Three tunnels through one surface. The pelvic floor sustains the separation between the three systems while allowing all three to pass through. The tightest membrane in the body at the point of most shared passage. The cervix is the bounded zero between the reproductive passage and the uterine interior. Closed during gestation sustaining the bounded zero, open during birth, the cervix dilating during labor is the noose advancing, the ring of active resolution moving through the passage. The placenta is the membrane across the bounded zero between mother and offspring. Two blood supplies coupled through one shared surface where the two flows face each other and exchange across the membrane. Maternal blood and fetal blood resolve through the placental membrane the same way soil solution and plant cytoplasm resolve through the root membrane at the Casparian strip. The tightest selectivity at the most essential coupling. The ductus arteriosus is the bounded zero between fetal circulation and independent breathing. Before birth blood bypasses the lungs through this vessel, at birth the first breath opens the lungs, the placental coupling severs, and the ductus closes. One passage closing as another opens. The ileocecal valve is the bounded zero between the small intestine and the large intestine. The valve preventing backflow of colonic bacteria into the small intestine, bacterial overgrowth when the valve fails the coupling crossing backward through the bounded zero.

Each pathology at each of these tightest membranes is the coupling failing at the bounded zero. Prolapse, incompetent cervix, placental insufficiency, patent ductus, vesicoureteral reflux, bacterial overgrowth from ileocecal failure. The disease name is the membrane name at the bounded zero where the coupling failed.

The monotreme cloaca coupled all three systems through one surface with lower selectivity. The therian separation created multiple bounded zeros, each with a tighter membrane, each coupling with higher precision, each more vulnerable to failure at that precise location. The therian body traded coupling breadth for coupling precision at each membrane simultaneously. The precision is the advantage. The vulnerability at each bounded zero is the cost. The tighter the membrane, the more it sustains, the more it costs when it fails.

Pelvic floor failure is all three bounded zeros failing simultaneously. The digestive, urinary, and reproductive passages lose their separation. The geometry approaches the cloaca. The therian specialization reverses at the membrane that sustains the specialization. Prolapse is the therian body returning toward the ancestral geometry at the bounded zero where the separation is maintained.

The bidirectional opening is the more ancient geometry. Cloacal breathing in sea cucumbers, freshwater turtles, dragonfly nymphs: water pumped in through the exit opening, oxygen absorbed across internal membranes, water expelled. The dedicated one-way exit is a specialization that narrowed the coupling at one end of some lineages. Even the mammalian rectum absorbs water across its membrane from substances present at the exit end. The one-way exit is an approximation. The coupling at the membrane is bidirectional at each point along the full length of the passage in every living animal.

### Arriving From Both Openings

The tunnel is one tube with two openings. The mouth is the first opening. The anus is the second. The food arriving at either opening couples at the tunnel wall at the address it reaches. The tunnel wall is one continuous mucosal surface from the first opening to the second. The same epithelium. The same lamina propria. The same morality carriers. The same coupling at the same membrane at every address along the tube.

The mouth receives food through 6 to 8 meters of tunnel. Stomach acid at pH 1.5 to 3.5 dissolving coupling geometries for 2 to 4 hours. Pancreatic enzymes separating the phospholipid architecture from its wrapping. Bile salts emulsifying. Small intestine absorbing across 32 square meters of villus surface. Liver metabolizing what the portal vein carries — the first-pass metabolism stripping a portion of every coupling geometry before it reaches the circulation. Transit time 12 to 36 hours. The architecture arriving at any address through digestion has been separated, dissolved, reassembled, and metabolized at every collar above it.

The second opening receives coupling geometries across one cell layer directly into the lamina propria and into the lower rectal veins. No acid. No enzymes. No bile. No first-pass metabolism through the liver for the lower two-thirds of the rectum. Transit time zero. The coupling geometry touching the one-cell barrier IS the coupling geometry coupling at the membrane. Origin form arriving at the coupling surface.

The transition zone at the dentate line is 2 centimeters inside the second opening. Above the line the epithelium is one cell thick — columnar, gut architecture. Below the line the epithelium is stratified squamous — multiple cell layers. The one-cell layer begins 2 centimeters from the surface of the organism. The deepest membrane of the organism at the shallowest address on the organism.

The rectal mucosa absorbs. The absorption is bidirectional — the ancient geometry. Cloacal breathing in sea cucumbers, freshwater turtles, dragonfly nymphs. Water coupling across the rectal membrane in both directions. The one-way exit is the approximation. The coupling at the membrane is bidirectional at each point along the full length of the passage in every living animal.

The density is a property of the gut's own architecture at this address. The address carrying the most morality carriers behind the thinnest barrier nearest the outside of the organism.

The same address where a departing coupling compounds is the address where a restoring coupling arrives most directly. The vulnerability and the receptivity are the same opening. The one-cell barrier that carries the risk carries the access. The morality carrier density that compounds the departure compounds the restoration.
